6306   // Initialization
6307   void generate_initial() {
6308     // Generates all stubs and initializes the entry points
6309 
6310     // This platform-specific settings are needed by generate_call_stub()
6311     create_control_words();
6312 
6313     // entry points that exist in all platforms Note: This is code
6314     // that could be shared among different platforms - however the
6315     // benefit seems to be smaller than the disadvantage of having a
6316     // much more complicated generator structure. See also comment in
6317     // stubRoutines.hpp.
6318 
6319     StubRoutines::_forward_exception_entry = generate_forward_exception();
6320 
6321     StubRoutines::_call_stub_entry =
6322       generate_call_stub(StubRoutines::_call_stub_return_address);



6323 
6324     // is referenced by megamorphic call
6325     StubRoutines::_catch_exception_entry = generate_catch_exception();
6326 
6327     // atomic calls
6328     StubRoutines::_atomic_xchg_entry          = generate_atomic_xchg();
6329     StubRoutines::_atomic_xchg_long_entry     = generate_atomic_xchg_long();
6330     StubRoutines::_atomic_cmpxchg_entry       = generate_atomic_cmpxchg();
6331     StubRoutines::_atomic_cmpxchg_byte_entry  = generate_atomic_cmpxchg_byte();
6332     StubRoutines::_atomic_cmpxchg_long_entry  = generate_atomic_cmpxchg_long();
6333     StubRoutines::_atomic_add_entry           = generate_atomic_add();
6334     StubRoutines::_atomic_add_long_entry      = generate_atomic_add_long();
6335     StubRoutines::_fence_entry                = generate_orderaccess_fence();
6336 
6337     // platform dependent
6338     StubRoutines::x86::_get_previous_fp_entry = generate_get_previous_fp();
6339     StubRoutines::x86::_get_previous_sp_entry = generate_get_previous_sp();
6340 
6341     StubRoutines::x86::_verify_mxcsr_entry    = generate_verify_mxcsr();
6342 
6343     StubRoutines::x86::_f2i_fixup             = generate_f2i_fixup();
6344     StubRoutines::x86::_f2l_fixup             = generate_f2l_fixup();
6345     StubRoutines::x86::_d2i_fixup             = generate_d2i_fixup();
6346     StubRoutines::x86::_d2l_fixup             = generate_d2l_fixup();
6347 
6348     StubRoutines::x86::_float_sign_mask       = generate_fp_mask("float_sign_mask",  0x7FFFFFFF7FFFFFFF);
6349     StubRoutines::x86::_float_sign_flip       = generate_fp_mask("float_sign_flip",  0x8000000080000000);
6350     StubRoutines::x86::_double_sign_mask      = generate_fp_mask("double_sign_mask", 0x7FFFFFFFFFFFFFFF);
6351     StubRoutines::x86::_double_sign_flip      = generate_fp_mask("double_sign_flip", 0x8000000000000000);
6352 
6353     // Build this early so it's available for the interpreter.
6354     StubRoutines::_throw_StackOverflowError_entry =
6355       generate_throw_exception("StackOverflowError throw_exception",
6356                                CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address,
6357                                                 SharedRuntime::
6358                                                 throw_StackOverflowError));
6359     StubRoutines::_throw_delayed_StackOverflowError_entry =
6360       generate_throw_exception("delayed StackOverflowError throw_exception",
6361                                CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address,
6362                                                 SharedRuntime::
6363                                                 throw_delayed_StackOverflowError));
6364     if (UseCRC32Intrinsics) {
6365       // set table address before stub generation which use it
6366       StubRoutines::_crc_table_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_crc_table;
6367       StubRoutines::_updateBytesCRC32 = generate_updateBytesCRC32();
6368     }
6369 
6370     if (UseCRC32CIntrinsics) {
6371       bool supports_clmul = VM_Version::supports_clmul();
6372       StubRoutines::x86::generate_CRC32C_table(supports_clmul);
6373       StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_crc32c_table;
6374       StubRoutines::_updateBytesCRC32C = generate_updateBytesCRC32C(supports_clmul);
6375     }
6376     if (UseLibmIntrinsic && InlineIntrinsics) {
6377       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dsin) ||
6378           vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dcos) ||
6379           vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dtan)) {
6380         StubRoutines::x86::_ONEHALF_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_ONEHALF;
6381         StubRoutines::x86::_P_2_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_P_2;
6382         StubRoutines::x86::_SC_4_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_SC_4;
6383         StubRoutines::x86::_Ctable_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_Ctable;
6384         StubRoutines::x86::_SC_2_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_SC_2;
6385         StubRoutines::x86::_SC_3_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_SC_3;
6386         StubRoutines::x86::_SC_1_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_SC_1;
6387         StubRoutines::x86::_PI_INV_TABLE_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_PI_INV_TABLE;
6388         StubRoutines::x86::_PI_4_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_PI_4;
6389         StubRoutines::x86::_PI32INV_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_PI32INV;
6390         StubRoutines::x86::_SIGN_MASK_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_SIGN_MASK;
6391         StubRoutines::x86::_P_1_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_P_1;
6392         StubRoutines::x86::_P_3_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_P_3;
6393         StubRoutines::x86::_NEG_ZERO_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_NEG_ZERO;
6394       }
6395       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dexp)) {
6396         StubRoutines::_dexp = generate_libmExp();
6397       }
6398       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dlog)) {
6399         StubRoutines::_dlog = generate_libmLog();
6400       }
6401       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dlog10)) {
6402         StubRoutines::_dlog10 = generate_libmLog10();
6403       }
6404       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dpow)) {
6405         StubRoutines::_dpow = generate_libmPow();
6406       }
6407       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dsin)) {
6408         StubRoutines::_dsin = generate_libmSin();
6409       }
6410       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dcos)) {
6411         StubRoutines::_dcos = generate_libmCos();
6412       }
6413       if (vmIntrinsics::is_intrinsic_available(vmIntrinsics::_dtan)) {
6414         StubRoutines::_dtan = generate_libmTan();
6415       }
6416     }
6417 
6418     // Safefetch stubs.
6419     generate_safefetch("SafeFetch32", sizeof(int),     &StubRoutines::_safefetch32_entry,
6420                                                        &StubRoutines::_safefetch32_fault_pc,
6421                                                        &StubRoutines::_safefetch32_continuation_pc);
6422     generate_safefetch("SafeFetchN", sizeof(intptr_t), &StubRoutines::_safefetchN_entry,
6423                                                        &StubRoutines::_safefetchN_fault_pc,
6424                                                        &StubRoutines::_safefetchN_continuation_pc);
6425   }
6426 
6427   void generate_all() {
6428     // Generates all stubs and initializes the entry points
6429 
6430     // These entry points require SharedInfo::stack0 to be set up in
6431     // non-core builds and need to be relocatable, so they each
6432     // fabricate a RuntimeStub internally.
6433     StubRoutines::_throw_AbstractMethodError_entry =
6434       generate_throw_exception("AbstractMethodError throw_exception",
6435                                CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address,
6436                                                 SharedRuntime::
6437                                                 throw_AbstractMethodError));
6438 
6439     StubRoutines::_throw_IncompatibleClassChangeError_entry =
6440       generate_throw_exception("IncompatibleClassChangeError throw_exception",
6441                                CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address,
6442                                                 SharedRuntime::
6443                                                 throw_IncompatibleClassChangeError));
6444 
6445     StubRoutines::_throw_NullPointerException_at_call_entry =
6446       generate_throw_exception("NullPointerException at call throw_exception",
6447                                CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address,
6448                                                 SharedRuntime::
6449                                                 throw_NullPointerException_at_call));
6450 
6451     // entry points that are platform specific
6452     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_float_sign_mask = generate_vector_mask("vector_float_sign_mask", 0x7FFFFFFF7FFFFFFF);
6453     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_float_sign_flip = generate_vector_mask("vector_float_sign_flip", 0x8000000080000000);
6454     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_double_sign_mask = generate_vector_mask("vector_double_sign_mask", 0x7FFFFFFFFFFFFFFF);
6455     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_double_sign_flip = generate_vector_mask("vector_double_sign_flip", 0x8000000000000000);
6456     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_short_to_byte_mask = generate_vector_mask("vector_short_to_byte_mask", 0x00ff00ff00ff00ff);
6457     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_byte_perm_mask = generate_vector_byte_perm_mask("vector_byte_perm_mask");
6458     StubRoutines::x86::_vector_long_sign_mask = generate_vector_mask("vector_long_sign_mask", 0x8000000000000000);
6459 
6460     // support for verify_oop (must happen after universe_init)
6461     StubRoutines::_verify_oop_subroutine_entry = generate_verify_oop();
6462 
6463     // data cache line writeback
6464     StubRoutines::_data_cache_writeback = generate_data_cache_writeback();
6465     StubRoutines::_data_cache_writeback_sync = generate_data_cache_writeback_sync();
6466 
6467     // arraycopy stubs used by compilers
6468     generate_arraycopy_stubs();
6469 
6470     // don't bother generating these AES intrinsic stubs unless global flag is set
6471     if (UseAESIntrinsics) {
6472       StubRoutines::x86::_key_shuffle_mask_addr = generate_key_shuffle_mask();  // needed by the others
6473       StubRoutines::_aescrypt_encryptBlock = generate_aescrypt_encryptBlock();
6474       StubRoutines::_aescrypt_decryptBlock = generate_aescrypt_decryptBlock();
6475       StubRoutines::_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt = generate_cipherBlockChaining_encryptAESCrypt();
6476       if (VM_Version::supports_avx512_vaes() &&  VM_Version::supports_avx512vl() && VM_Version::supports_avx512dq() ) {
6477         StubRoutines::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt = generate_cipherBlockChaining_decryptVectorAESCrypt();
6478         StubRoutines::_electronicCodeBook_encryptAESCrypt = generate_electronicCodeBook_encryptAESCrypt();
6479         StubRoutines::_electronicCodeBook_decryptAESCrypt = generate_electronicCodeBook_decryptAESCrypt();
6480       } else {
6481         StubRoutines::_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt = generate_cipherBlockChaining_decryptAESCrypt_Parallel();
6482       }
6483     }
6484     if (UseAESCTRIntrinsics) {
6485       if (VM_Version::supports_avx512_vaes() && VM_Version::supports_avx512bw() && VM_Version::supports_avx512vl()) {
6486         StubRoutines::x86::_counter_mask_addr = counter_mask_addr();
6487         StubRoutines::_counterMode_AESCrypt = generate_counterMode_VectorAESCrypt();
6488       } else {
6489         StubRoutines::x86::_counter_shuffle_mask_addr = generate_counter_shuffle_mask();
6490         StubRoutines::_counterMode_AESCrypt = generate_counterMode_AESCrypt_Parallel();
6491       }
6492     }
6493 
6494     if (UseSHA1Intrinsics) {
6495       StubRoutines::x86::_upper_word_mask_addr = generate_upper_word_mask();
6496       StubRoutines::x86::_shuffle_byte_flip_mask_addr = generate_shuffle_byte_flip_mask();
6497       StubRoutines::_sha1_implCompress = generate_sha1_implCompress(false, "sha1_implCompress");
6498       StubRoutines::_sha1_implCompressMB = generate_sha1_implCompress(true, "sha1_implCompressMB");
6499     }
6500     if (UseSHA256Intrinsics) {
6501       StubRoutines::x86::_k256_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_k256;
6502       char* dst = (char*)StubRoutines::x86::_k256_W;
6503       char* src = (char*)StubRoutines::x86::_k256;
6504       for (int ii = 0; ii < 16; ++ii) {
6505         memcpy(dst + 32 * ii,      src + 16 * ii, 16);
6506         memcpy(dst + 32 * ii + 16, src + 16 * ii, 16);
6507       }
6508       StubRoutines::x86::_k256_W_adr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_k256_W;
6509       StubRoutines::x86::_pshuffle_byte_flip_mask_addr = generate_pshuffle_byte_flip_mask();
6510       StubRoutines::_sha256_implCompress = generate_sha256_implCompress(false, "sha256_implCompress");
6511       StubRoutines::_sha256_implCompressMB = generate_sha256_implCompress(true, "sha256_implCompressMB");
6512     }
6513     if (UseSHA512Intrinsics) {
6514       StubRoutines::x86::_k512_W_addr = (address)StubRoutines::x86::_k512_W;
6515       StubRoutines::x86::_pshuffle_byte_flip_mask_addr_sha512 = generate_pshuffle_byte_flip_mask_sha512();
6516       StubRoutines::_sha512_implCompress = generate_sha512_implCompress(false, "sha512_implCompress");
6517       StubRoutines::_sha512_implCompressMB = generate_sha512_implCompress(true, "sha512_implCompressMB");
6518     }
6519 
6520     // Generate GHASH intrinsics code
6521     if (UseGHASHIntrinsics) {
6522     StubRoutines::x86::_ghash_long_swap_mask_addr = generate_ghash_long_swap_mask();
6523     StubRoutines::x86::_ghash_byte_swap_mask_addr = generate_ghash_byte_swap_mask();
6524       if (VM_Version::supports_avx()) {
6525         StubRoutines::x86::_ghash_shuffmask_addr = ghash_shufflemask_addr();
6526         StubRoutines::x86::_ghash_poly_addr = ghash_polynomial_addr();
6527         StubRoutines::_ghash_processBlocks = generate_avx_ghash_processBlocks();
6528       } else {
6529         StubRoutines::_ghash_processBlocks = generate_ghash_processBlocks();
6530       }
6531     }
6532 
6533     if (UseBASE64Intrinsics) {
6534       StubRoutines::x86::_and_mask = base64_and_mask_addr();
6535       StubRoutines::x86::_bswap_mask = base64_bswap_mask_addr();
6536       StubRoutines::x86::_base64_charset = base64_charset_addr();
6537       StubRoutines::x86::_url_charset = base64url_charset_addr();
6538       StubRoutines::x86::_gather_mask = base64_gather_mask_addr();
6539       StubRoutines::x86::_left_shift_mask = base64_left_shift_mask_addr();
6540       StubRoutines::x86::_right_shift_mask = base64_right_shift_mask_addr();
6541       StubRoutines::_base64_encodeBlock = generate_base64_encodeBlock();
6542     }
6543 
6544     BarrierSetNMethod* bs_nm = BarrierSet::barrier_set()->barrier_set_nmethod();
6545     if (bs_nm != NULL) {
6546       StubRoutines::x86::_method_entry_barrier = generate_method_entry_barrier();
6547     }
6548 #ifdef COMPILER2
6549     if (UseMultiplyToLenIntrinsic) {
6550       StubRoutines::_multiplyToLen = generate_multiplyToLen();
6551     }
6552     if (UseSquareToLenIntrinsic) {
6553       StubRoutines::_squareToLen = generate_squareToLen();
6554     }
6555     if (UseMulAddIntrinsic) {
6556       StubRoutines::_mulAdd = generate_mulAdd();
6557     }
6558     if (VM_Version::supports_avx512_vbmi2()) {
6559       StubRoutines::_bigIntegerRightShiftWorker = generate_bigIntegerRightShift();
6560       StubRoutines::_bigIntegerLeftShiftWorker = generate_bigIntegerLeftShift();
6561     }
6562 #ifndef _WINDOWS
6563     if (UseMontgomeryMultiplyIntrinsic) {
6564       StubRoutines::_montgomeryMultiply
6565         = CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, SharedRuntime::montgomery_multiply);
6566     }
6567     if (UseMontgomerySquareIntrinsic) {
6568       StubRoutines::_montgomerySquare
6569         = CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, SharedRuntime::montgomery_square);
6570     }
6571 #endif // WINDOWS
6572 #endif // COMPILER2
6573 
6574     if (UseVectorizedMismatchIntrinsic) {
6575       StubRoutines::_vectorizedMismatch = generate_vectorizedMismatch();
6576     }
6577   }
6578 
6579  public:
6580   StubGenerator(CodeBuffer* code, bool all) : StubCodeGenerator(code) {
6581     if (all) {
6582       generate_all();
6583     } else {
6584       generate_initial();
6585     }
6586   }
6587 }; // end class declaration
6588 
6589 #define UCM_TABLE_MAX_ENTRIES 16
6590 void StubGenerator_generate(CodeBuffer* code, bool all) {
6591   if (UnsafeCopyMemory::_table == NULL) {
6592     UnsafeCopyMemory::create_table(UCM_TABLE_MAX_ENTRIES);
6593   }
6594   StubGenerator g(code, all);
6595 }
